)@@G@@* BIT 31 OF THE RUN'S CONDITION WORD IS SET IF THIS RUN IS A RESTART    HB
)@@G@@@F@@@@      * AFTER A SYSTEM CRASH, I.E. DUE TO THE @RUN R-SUBOPTION.   HC
)@@G@@@G@@@@      * WE MUST MAKE AN ASSUMPTION AS TO WHETHER THE RUN CAUGHT INHD
)@@G@@ THE  @H@@@@      * CRASH HAD OR HAD NOT DONE THE @START IN THIS PARAGRAHE
)@@G@@PH BEFORE THE     @G@@@@      * CRASH.   AS SECRUN EXECUTION IS ALMOST AHF
)@@G@@LWAYS SHORTER THAN THE  @G@@@@      * PHASE 2 SECURE ECL, IT IS MORE PROHG
)@@G@@BABLE THAT THE @START WAS     @F@@@@      * DONE.  SO IF THIS IS A RESTAHH
)@@G@@RT, DON'T DO ANOTHER @START.  @@@@@@@B@@@@           CALL 'COND' USING CHI
)@@G@@OND-WORD.   @B@@@@           IF COND-RESTART-BIT NOT = 0    @ @@@@      HJ
)@@G@@         GO TO BS-999.  @@@@@@@A@@@@           IF DAY-OF-WEEK = 'SAT'   HK
)@@G@@@ @@@@               GO TO BS-300.  @@@@@@@G@@@@      * MONDAY THRU FRIDHL
)@@G@@AY: RUNS 8 A.M. TO 11 P.M. THEN START NEXT DAY  @@@@@@@^@@@@           IHM
)@@G@@F TW-HH < 23@D@@@@               ADD 1 TW-HH GIVING SECRUN-START-TIME   HN
)@@G@@@#@@@@           ELSE   @C@@@@               MOVE 8 TO SECRUN-START-TIMEHO
)@@G@@.     @^@@@@           GO TO BS-400.@@@@@@@D@@@@      * SATURDAY: RUNS 8HP
)@@G@@ A.M. TO 4 P.M. THEN DIES.    @@@@@@@#@@@@       BS-300.    @^@@@@      HQ
)@@G@@     IF TW-HH < 16@D@@@@               ADD 1 TW-HH GIVING SECRUN-START-THR
)@@G@@IME   @ @@@@               GO TO BS-400   @#@@@@           ELSE   @ @@@@HS

)@@G@@RUN-STARTCARD     @ @@@@               GO TO BS-999.  @E@@@@           CHV

)@@G@@@F@@@4      *    WRITTEN BY RICHARD STRANGE - SDC/ISI RTP NOVEMBER 1980 IB
)@@G@@@@@@@4@G@@@4      *    THIS PROGRAM READS THE FILE SEC-USERS CONTAINING IC
)@@G@@BACKED UP   @G@@@4      *    REQUESTS FROM THE USER COMMUNITY FOR FILE RID
)@@G@@ECOVERY.  THE     @H@@@4      *    PROGRAM BUILDS AND @STARTS A SECURE RIE
)@@G@@UNSTREAM TO CARRY OUT THE     @G@@@4      *    RECOVERY.   IT ALSO LISTSIF

)@@G@@@H@@@4      *            SETTING) FILES IN SEC-USERS BY STARTING ANOTHERIK

)@@G@@(@ADD OF    @D@@@4      *            SECURE ECL) LOST IN MACHINE-CRASH  IO

)@@G@@*            DUE TO @PACK OF PF USER*RUNSTREAM WHICH CONTAINED SECRUN ELIU
)@@G@@T)    @I@@@4      * LEVEL 3.2: NO START OF RECOVERY RUN (45FILZ) FROM COIV
)@@G@@NTINUATION RUN (45FIL1) @I@@@4      *            HISTORY KEYS IN START-FIW
)@@G@@ILE (FOR 45FILZ) INSTEAD OF PRINT-FILE    @H@@@4      * LEVEL 3.3: PHASEIX

)@@G@@      * LEVEL 4.2: IGNORES TWO ADJACENT, IDENTICAL FILENAMES ON 'LOAD FIJI

)@@G@@@G@@@4      * SORT-ORDER EXPLANATION: (1) SORT-OFILE - TO SEPARATE SECURSR
)@@G@@E AND @G@@@4      * READER LOADS: IF OFILE NOT LOW-VALUES, READER WILL BSS
)@@G@@E USED TO   @C@@@4      * LOAD THE FILE INTO THE NAMED OUTPUT AREA@H@@@4ST
)@@G@@      * (2) TAPE1 - TO GET ALL FILES ON THE SAME TAPE TOGETHER SO WE GENSU
)@@G@@ERATE @F@@@4      * ONE SECURE/READER EXECUTION ONLY (I.E. RUN) FOR EACHSV
)@@G@@ TAPE @I@@@4      * (3) TAPE2 - SO THAT DOUBLE TAPE LOADS COME AFTER ALLSW
)@@G@@ SINGLE TAPE ENTRIES    @H@@@4      * FOR A GIVEN TAPE1 (I.E. IF WE HAD SX
)@@G@@SEC123,SEC123+SEC124,SEC123 THIS    @H@@@4      * MUST BE SORTED TO SEC1SY
)@@G@@23,SEC123,SEC123+SEC124 SINCE THE DOUBLE TAPE   @I@@@4      * GETS ITS OSZ
)@@G@@WN RUN AND WITHOUT THE SORT THERE WOULD BE 3 RUNS INSTEAD OF 2    @H@@@4TA
)@@G@@      * AFTER THE SORT - RUN1=THE 2 FILES ON SEC123 ALONE,RUN2=SEC123+SETB
)@@G@@C124) @H@@@4      * (4) FILENAME - SO THAT IF A FILE IS ENTERED TWICE WITC
)@@G@@TH THE SAME TAPE  @G@@@4      * THE DUPLICATION CAN BE ELIMINATED (IN BCTD
)@@G@@-100) THUS AVOIDING     @G@@@4      * THE 'FILE NOT FOUND' ERROR WHEN 'STE
)@@G@@ECURE' TRIES TO FIND THE FILE @A@@@4      * FURTHER DOWN THE SAME TAPE  TF
)@@G@@@@@@@4@B@@@4           SORT SORT-IN ASCENDING KEY     @F@@@4            TG

)@@G@@@^@@@5      ***************   @@@@@4@H@@@4      * GENERATES ECL TO ALTERGF

)@@G@@REFERENCED ENTRY IS CHANGED TO THE TIME WHEN 'CHGREF' IS    @H@@@4      GH
)@@G@@* EXECUTED.   THIS PREVENTS THE RELOADED FILE FROM BEING ROLLED-OUT     GI
)@@G@@@F@@@4      * OR ARCHIVED IMMEDIATELY.  THIS WOULD HAPPEN IF THE OLD    GJ
)@@G@@@I@@@4      * TIME-LAST-REFERENCED FROM THE BACKUP-TAPE MFD-DATA WERE LEGK

)@@G@@SE    @ @@@U               GO TO BR-250.  @ @@@U           IF WS-P-USE =ER
)@@G@@ 'SA' @B@@@U               MOVE 'SAVE ALL' TO WS-P-USE@ @@@U            ES
)@@G@@   GO TO BR-250.  @ @@@U           IF WS-P-USE = 'RM' @B@@@U            ET
)@@G@@   MOVE 'REMOVE' TO WS-P-USE  @ @@@U               GO TO BR-250.  @ @@@UEU
)@@G@@           IF WS-P-USE = 'ST' @C@@@U               MOVE 'SECTAPEMOD' TO EV
)@@G@@WS-P-USE    @ @@@U               GO TO BR-250.  @ @@@U           IF WS-PEW
)@@G@@-USE = 'BU' @C@@@U               MOVE 'SECBCKUPCHEK' TO WS-P-USE. @@@@@UEX
)@@G@@@#@@@U       BR-250.    @A@@@U           WRITE PREC FROM WS-PREC3.@@@@@UEY
)@@G@@@#@@@U       BR-260.    @B@@@U           MOVE PB-DATE TO TAPE-PBDATE.   EZ
)@@G@@@C@@@U           MOVE RUN-DATE-TIME TO TAPE-DATE.     @B@@@U           MFA
)@@G@@OVE JULIAN-CNT TO TAPE-JULIAN.@E@@@U           REWRITE TAPE-RECORD  INVAFB
)@@G@@LID KEY GO TO BR-910.   @^@@@U           GO TO BR-200.@@@@@U@#@@@U      FC
)@@G@@ BR-300.    @B@@@U           IF NEW-DOUBLE-TAPE-COUNT = 0   @ @@@U      FD
)@@G@@         GO TO BR-999.  @A@@@U           MOVE SPACES TO WS-PREC1. @F@@@UFE
)@@G@@           MOVE 'TAPES USED WITH CONTINUATION REELS IN THIS RUN'  @ @@@UFF
)@@G@@               TO WS-PREC12.  @C@@@U           WRITE PREC FROM WS-PREC1 FG
)@@G@@AFTER 3.    @A@@@U           MOVE SPACES TO PREC.     @^@@@U           WFH
)@@G@@RITE PREC.  @@@@@U@A@@@U           SET SUB TO D-TAPE-INDEX. @A@@@U      FI
)@@G@@     SUBTRACT 1 FROM SUB.     @A@@@U           SET D-TAPE-INDEX TO 1.   FJ
)@@G@@@C@@@U           PERFORM BR-400 THRU BR-499 SUB TIMES.@^@@@U           GFK
)@@G@@O TO BR-999.@@@@@U@#@@@U       BR-400.    @C@@@U           MOVE D-TAPE1(FL
)@@G@@D-TAPE-INDEX) TO DUMP1. @C@@@U           MOVE D-TAPE2(D-TAPE-INDEX) TO DFM
)@@G@@UMP2. @G@@@U           DISPLAY BLANKING DUMP2 ' USED AS A CONTINUATION RFN
)@@G@@EEL TO '    @D@@@U               DUMP1 ' IN THIS RUN' UPON PRINTER.     FO
)@@G@@@#@@@U       BR-499.    @A@@@U           SET D-TAPE-INDEX UP BY 1.@@@@@UFP
)@@G@@@#@@@U       BR-900.    @F@@@U           EXHIBIT NAMED '*ERROR* BR-000 IFQ
)@@G@@NVALID KEY ON READ'     @C@@@U               T-STATUS TAPE-NAME TAPE-RECFR
)@@G@@ORD.  @^@@@U           GO TO BR-999.@@@@@U@#@@@U       BR-910.    @F@@@UFS
)@@G@@           EXHIBIT NAMED '*ERROR* BR-250 INVALID KEY ON REWRITE'  @A@@@UFT
)@@G@@               T-STATUS TAPE-RECORD.@@@@@U@#@@@U       BR-999.    @#@@@UFU
)@@G@@           EXIT.  @]@@@U      /     @A@@@U       BT-CHECK-DOUBLES SECTIOFV
)@@G@@N 51. @A@@@U      ***************************   @@@@@U@G@@@U      * CHECFW
)@@G@@K IF ANY OF THE PRE-EXISTING DOUBLE-TAPE PAIRS HAVE BEEN    @G@@@U      FX
)@@G@@* INVALIDATED BY THE RE-USE OF ONE OF THE PAIR OF TAPES DURING    @^@@@UFY
)@@G@@      * THIS UPDATE.    @@@@@U@#@@@U       BT-000.    @ @@@U           MFZ
)@@G@@OVE 0 TO TAPE-KEY.@D@@@U           READ SEC-TAPES  INVALID KEY GO TO BT-GA
)@@G@@900.  @D@@@U           REWRITE TAPE-RECORD FROM TAPE-HEADER-RECORD@B@@@UGB
)@@G@@               INVALID KEY GO TO BT-900.  @@@@@U@#@@@U       BT-100.    GC
)@@G@@@B@@@U           READ SEC-TAPES NEXT RECORD     @A@@@U               AT GD
)@@G@@END GO TO BT-999. @A@@@U           IF TAPE-DT-FLAG = SPACES @ @@@U      GE
)@@G@@         GO TO BT-100.  @D@@@U           MOVE TAPE-RECORD TO WS-DOUBLE-TGF
)@@G@@APE-REC.    @B@@@U           MOVE WS-DT1-KEY TO TAPE-KEY.   @ @@@U      GG
)@@G@@     PERFORM BT-500.    @B@@@U           MOVE WS-DT2-KEY TO TAPE-KEY.   GH
)@@G@@@ @@@U           PERFORM BT-500.    @B@@@U           MOVE WS-DT-KEY TO TGI
)@@G@@APE-KEY.    @D@@@U           READ SEC-TAPES  INVALID KEY GO TO BT-900.  GJ
)@@G@@@ @@@U           IF WS-DT-PBDATE = 0@E@@@U               REWRITE TAPE-REGK
)@@G@@CORD FROM WS-DOUBLE-TAPE-REC  @C@@@U                   INVALID KEY GO TOGL
)@@G@@ BT-900.    @^@@@U           GO TO BT-100.@@@@@U@#@@@U       BT-200.    GM

)@@G@@TO BT-999.  @ @@@U           ADD 1 TO TAPE-KEY. @D@@@U           START SGO
)@@G@@EC-TAPES  INVALID KEY GO TO BT-900. @^@@@U           GO TO BT-100.@@@@@UGP
)@@G@@@#@@@U       BT-500.    @D@@@U           READ SEC-TAPES  INVALID KEY GO GQ
)@@G@@TO BT-900.  @C@@@U           IF TAPE-PBDATE NOT = WS-DT-PBDATE    @D@@@UGR

)@@G@@   MOVE 1 TO NEW-TAPE-FLAG.   @@@@@U@#@@@U       BT-900.    @E@@@U      GT

)@@G@@ BT-999.    @ @@@U           CLOSE SEC-TAPES.   @]@@@U      /     @A@@@UGW
)@@G@@       BZ-TERMINATE SECTION 51.     @ @@@U      *********************** GX
)@@G@@@@@@@U@#@@@U       BZ-000.    @B@@@U           MOVE ERROR-COUNT TO WS-PRGY
)@@G@@EC11. @D@@@U           MOVE 'ERRORS AT PROGRAM END' TO WS-PREC12. @D@@@UGZ
)@@G@@           WRITE PREC FROM WS-PREC1 AFTER 2 LINES.    @^@@@U           CHA

)@@G@@EROGATE. IF THE INCORRECT NUMBER    @F@@@@. OF ARGUMENTS IS PASSED TO THRJ
)@@G@@E ROUTINE THEN IT WILL ABORT WITH   @]@@@@. A MESSAGE.@[@@@@.     @ @@@@RK
)@@G@@. CALLING SEQUENCE FROM COBOL:@F@@@@.     CALL 'SORTF' USING NO-RECORDS,RL
)@@G@@       . 01 LEVEL S9(10) COMP @F@@@@.                        RECORD-SIZERM
)@@G@@,      . 01 LEV S9(10) COMP   @F@@@@.                        RETUR$-CODERN
)@@G@@,      . 01 LEV S9(10) COMP   @H@@@@.                        OPTION-LISTRO
)@@G@@.      . 01 LEV S9(10) COMP (OPTIONAL)    @A@@@@.     IF RETUR$-CODE NOTRP
)@@G@@ EQUAL ZERO @ @@@@.       THEN SORTF FAILED .   @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. THE RQ
)@@G@@RECORD-SIZE IS IN ASCII CHARACTERS. FOR FIELDATA, SET OPTION-LIST @[@@@@RR
)@@G@@.     @E@@@@. MODIFIED 12/79 TO NOTIFY CONSOLE IF SPACE NOT AVAILABLE   RS
)@@G@@@G@@@@. TO A VALUE OF ONE. IF ASCII CHAR THEN OPTION-LIST IS NOT REQUIRERT
)@@G@@D.    @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * RU
)@@G@@* * * * * * * * * * *   @[@@@@.     @E@@@@          LXI,H1    A0,0,A0   RV
)@@G@@        . GET DBANK ADDRESS   @B@@@@          SSC       A0,18           RW
)@@G@@  .   @E@@@@         SX        X4,REGSAV$,A0       . SAVE REGISTER SET  RX
)@@G@@@A@@@@         SX        X5,REGSAV$+1,A0  @A@@@@         SX        X6,RERY
)@@G@@GSAV$+2,A0  @A@@@@         SX        X7,REGSAV$+3,A0  @A@@@@         SX RZ
)@@G@@       X8,REGSAV$+4,A0  @A@@@@         SX        X9,REGSAV$+5,A0  @A@@@@SA
)@@G@@         SX        X10,REGSAV$+6,A0 @A@@@@         SX        X11,REGSAV$SB
)@@G@@+7,A0 @A@@@@         DS        A0,REGSAV$+8,A0  @A@@@@         DS       SC
)@@G@@ A2,REGSAV$+10,A0 @A@@@@         DS        A4,REGSAV$+12,A0 @A@@@@      SD
)@@G@@   DS        A6,REGSAV$+14,A0 @A@@@@         DS        A8,REGSAV$+16,A0 SE
